+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)
+}

+func TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dependencies":{"@anthropic-ai/sdk":"^0.62.0"}}`))
+		case "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest":
+			http.Error(w, "github outage", http.StatusBadGateway)
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := svc.fetchVersions(context.Background())
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeSDKVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, codexVersion)
+}

+func newVersionFetcherTestService(t *testing.T, handler http.HandlerFunc) (*VersionFetcherService, *httptest.Server) {
+	t.Helper()
+
+	server := httptest.NewServer(handler)
+	svc := NewVersionFetcherService(clientidentity.NewRegistry(), &config.Config{})
+	svc.client = server.Client()
+	svc.npmURL = server.URL
+	svc.codexURL = server.URL + "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest"
+	return svc, server

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {

+	return http.DefaultClient

+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchNPMLatest(t *testing.T) {

+		})

+

+		assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", got)
+	})
+

+

+	})

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)
+}

+func TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":

+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dependencies":{"@anthropic-ai/sdk":"^0.62.0"}}`))
+		case "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest":
+			http.Error(w, "github outage", http.StatusBadGateway)
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := svc.fetchVersions(context.Background())
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeSDKVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, codexVersion)
+}

+func newVersionFetcherTestService(t *testing.T, handler http.HandlerFunc) (*VersionFetcherService, *httptest.Server) {
+	t.Helper()
+
+	server := httptest.NewServer(handler)
+	svc := NewVersionFetcherService(clientidentity.NewRegistry(), &config.Config{})
+	svc.client = server.Client()
+	svc.npmURL = server.URL
+	svc.codexURL = server.URL + "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest"
+	return svc, server

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
+	if err == nil {
+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }

+func TestFetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(t *testing.T) {
+	t.Run("returns dependency version and trims range prefix", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {

+		require.NoError(t, err)

+	})

+	t.Run("trims tilde range prefix", func(t *testing.T) {

+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		got, err := svc.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(context.Background(), "2.1.161")
+		require.NoError(t, err)
+		assert.Equal(t, "0.61.0", got)
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects missing sdk dependency", func(t *testing.T) {

+		defer server.Close()

+	})

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)
+}
+
+func TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dependencies":{"@anthropic-ai/sdk":"^0.62.0"}}`))
+		case "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest":
+			http.Error(w, "github outage", http.StatusBadGateway)
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := svc.fetchVersions(context.Background())
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeSDKVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, codexVersion)
+}

+func newVersionFetcherTestService(t *testing.T, handler http.HandlerFunc) (*VersionFetcherService, *httptest.Server) {
+	t.Helper()
+
+	server := httptest.NewServer(handler)
+	svc := NewVersionFetcherService(clientidentity.NewRegistry(), &config.Config{})
+	svc.client = server.Client()
+	svc.npmURL = server.URL
+	svc.codexURL = server.URL + "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest"
+	return svc, server
+}

 func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchVersions(ctx context.Context) (claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion string) {
-	_ = ctx
-	return "", "", ""
+	var wg sync.WaitGroup
+	var claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer string
+	var claudeErr, codexErr error
+
+	wg.Add(2)
+
+	go func() {
+		defer wg.Done()
+		claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, claudeErr = s.fetchClaudeVersions(ctx)
+	}()
+
+	go func() {
+		defer wg.Done()
+		codexVer, codexErr = s.fetchCodexVersion(ctx)
+	}()
+
+	wg.Wait()
+
+	if claudeErr != nil || codexErr != nil {
+		slog.Warn("version_fetcher_discard_update", "claude_error", claudeErr, "codex_error", codexErr)
+		return "", "", ""
+	}
+
+	return claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
+	if err == nil {
+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
 func (s *VersionFetcherService) buildClaudeHeaders(cliVer, sdkVer string) map[string]string {
 	return map[string]string{
 		"User-Agent":                  "claude-cli/" + cliVer + " (external, cli)",
@@ -116,3 +281,23 @@
 		"originator": "codex_cli_rs",
 	}
 }
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {
+		return s.client
+	}
+	return http.DefaultClient
+}
+
+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)

+func TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dependencies":{"@anthropic-ai/sdk":"^0.62.0"}}`))
+		case "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest":
+			http.Error(w, "github outage", http.StatusBadGateway)
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := svc.fetchVersions(context.Background())
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeSDKVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, codexVersion)
+}

+func newVersionFetcherTestService(t *testing.T, handler http.HandlerFunc) (*VersionFetcherService, *httptest.Server) {

+	svc.client = server.Client()

+	svc.codexURL = server.URL + "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest"
+	return svc, server

Also, I need to check if the scoped npm URL works correctly. Lastly, I want to ensure the version token patterns are extracting correctly, as I see various cases.
**Analyzing version requirements**

I see that the build metadata is being rejected because the task specifies a pure numeric version. However, the "release tag v0.125.0-beta.1" is causing issues with `release.Prerelease`. 

There's a situation where "npm latest and GitHub latest aren't in sync," but it seems there’s not much to do except address it fully. 

Regarding the UA suffix "buildCodexHeaders," currently, there’s no suffix for `codex_cli_rs/0.125`. Since the user mentioned needing a suffix for the version, it raises the question of whether we should update `buildCodexHeaders` to include this suffix. The user pointed out the R1 step2 fetchVersions implementation requires a specific suffix, but with pure numeric versions. It looks like I need to ensure `buildCodexHeaders` aligns properly in this context.
**Assessing UA version requirements**

The pitfall mentions that the UA requires OS/arch/terminal suffixes but that the version number should only consist of pure numeric values. This suggests that we shouldn't return the full UA version. However, if a dynamic update builds headers without the necessary suffix, it could lead to a situation where I'm not handling that trap correctly. I need to consider how to manage this dynamic aspect without compromising the versioning requirements.

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
+	if err == nil {
+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {
+		return s.client
+	}
+	return http.DefaultClient
+}
+
+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}

+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)

+func TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {

+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dependencies":{"@anthropic-ai/sdk":"^0.62.0"}}`))
+		case "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest":
+			http.Error(w, "github outage", http.StatusBadGateway)
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := svc.fetchVersions(context.Background())
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeSDKVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, codexVersion)

 func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchVersions(ctx context.Context) (claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion string) {

-	return "", "", ""
+	var wg sync.WaitGroup
+	var claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer string
+	var claudeErr, codexErr error
+
+	wg.Add(2)
+
+	go func() {
+		defer wg.Done()
+		claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, claudeErr = s.fetchClaudeVersions(ctx)
+	}()
+
+	go func() {
+		defer wg.Done()
+		codexVer, codexErr = s.fetchCodexVersion(ctx)
+	}()
+
+	wg.Wait()
+
+	if claudeErr != nil || codexErr != nil {
+		slog.Warn("version_fetcher_discard_update", "claude_error", claudeErr, "codex_error", codexErr)
+		return "", "", ""
+	}
+
+	return claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
+	if err == nil {
+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}

 	return map[string]string{

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {
+		return s.client
+	}
+	return http.DefaultClient
+}
+
+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

 func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchVersions(ctx context.Context) (claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion string) {

-	return "", "", ""

+	var claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer string
+	var claudeErr, codexErr error
+
+	wg.Add(2)
+
+	go func() {
+		defer wg.Done()
+		claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, claudeErr = s.fetchClaudeVersions(ctx)
+	}()
+
+	go func() {
+		defer wg.Done()
+		codexVer, codexErr = s.fetchCodexVersion(ctx)
+	}()
+
+	wg.Wait()
+

+		slog.Warn("version_fetcher_discard_update", "claude_error", claudeErr, "codex_error", codexErr)
+		return "", "", ""
+	}
+
+	return claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
+	if err == nil {
+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}

 		"originator": "codex_cli_rs",

 }

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {
+		return s.client
+	}
+	return http.DefaultClient
+}
+
+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchNPMLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	t.Run("returns latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+			assert.Equal(t, "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code", r.URL.Path)
+			assert.Equal(t, "application/json", r.Header.Get("Accept"))
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		got, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.NoError(t, err)
+		assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", got)
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects non 200", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {

+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.Error(t, err)
+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "npm registry status 404")
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects missing latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {

+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")

+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "no latest tag")
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects prerelease latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"3.0.0-beta.1"}}`))
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.Error(t, err)
+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "prerelease")
+	})
+

+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {

+			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusGatewayTimeout)
+		})

+

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {

+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {
+		return s.client
+	}
+	return http.DefaultClient

+
+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {

+	}

+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {

+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchNPMLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	t.Run("returns latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+			assert.Equal(t, "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code", r.URL.Path)

+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		got, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.NoError(t, err)
+		assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", got)
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects non 200", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
+			http.Error(w, "not found", http.StatusNotFound)
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.Error(t, err)
+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "npm registry status 404")
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects missing latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {

+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.Error(t, err)
+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "no latest tag")
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects prerelease latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {

+		})
+		defer server.Close()

+			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusGatewayTimeout)

+

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {

+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+

+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+

+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)
+}

+func TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dependencies":{"@anthropic-ai/sdk":"^0.62.0"}}`))
+		case "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest":
+			http.Error(w, "github outage", http.StatusBadGateway)
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := svc.fetchVersions(context.Background())
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeSDKVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, codexVersion)

+func newVersionFetcherTestService(t *testing.T, handler http.HandlerFunc) (*VersionFetcherService, *httptest.Server) {
+	t.Helper()
+
+	server := httptest.NewServer(handler)
+	svc := NewVersionFetcherService(clientidentity.NewRegistry(), &config.Config{})
+	svc.client = server.Client()
+	svc.npmURL = server.URL
+	svc.codexURL = server.URL + "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest"
+	return svc, server

     1	package service

     3	import (
     4		"context"

    17	
    18	const (
    19		defaultVersionFetchInterval = time.Hour
    20		versionFetchTimeout         = 30 * time.Second
    21		defaultNPMRegistryBaseURL   = "https://registry.npmjs.org"
    22		defaultCodexReleaseURL      = "https://api.github.com/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest"
    23	)
    24	
    25	type VersionFetcherService struct {
    26		registry *clientidentity.Registry
    27		cfg      *config.Config
    28		client   *http.Client
    29		npmURL   string
    30		codexURL string
    31		stopCh   chan struct{}
    32		stopOnce sync.Once
    33	}
    34	
    35	func NewVersionFetcherService(registry *clientidentity.Registry, cfg *config.Config) *VersionFetcherService {
    36		return &VersionFetcherService{
    37			registry: registry,
    38			cfg:      cfg,
    39			client:   http.DefaultClient,
    40			npmURL:   defaultNPMRegistryBaseURL,
    41			codexURL: defaultCodexReleaseURL,
    42			stopCh:   make(chan struct{}),
    43		}
    44	}
    45	
    46	// Start runs the periodic version fetch loop only when ua_auto_fetch is enabled.
    47	func (s *VersionFetcherService) Start() {
    48		if s == nil || s.cfg == nil || !s.cfg.Gateway.UAAutoFetch.Enabled {
    49			return
    50		}
    51	
    52		interval := s.cfg.Gateway.UAAutoFetch.Interval
    53		if interval == 0 {
    54			interval = defaultVersionFetchInterval
    55		}
    56	
    57		go func() {
    58			ticker := time.NewTicker(interval)
    59			defer ticker.Stop()
    60	
    61			for {
    62				select {
    63				case <-ticker.C:
    64					s.fetchAndUpdate()
    65				case <-s.stopCh:
    66					return
    67				}
    68			}
    69		}()
    70	}
    71	
    72	func (s *VersionFetcherService) Stop() {
    73		if s == nil {
    74			return
    75		}
    76		s.stopOnce.Do(func() {
    77			close(s.stopCh)
    78		})
    79	}
    80	
    81	func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchAndUpdate() {
    82		if s == nil || s.registry == nil {
    83			return
    84		}
    85	
    86		ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), versionFetchTimeout)
    87		defer cancel()
    88	
    89		claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := s.fetchVersions(ctx)
    90		if claudeVersion == "" || claudeSDKVersion == "" || codexVersion == "" {
    91			return
    92		}
    93	
    94		s.registry.Swap(&clientidentity.Snapshots{
    95			Claude: clientidentity.ClaudeSnapshot{
    96				Headers: s.buildClaudeHeaders(claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion),
    97				VersionFields: clientidentity.VersionFields{
    98					CLIVersion: claudeVersion,
    99					SDKVersion: claudeSDKVersion,
   100					CCVersion:  claudeVersion,
   101				},
   102				TLSProfileName: clientidentity.TLSProfileClaudeCLIDefault,
   103			},
   104			Codex: clientidentity.CodexSnapshot{
   105				Headers: s.buildCodexHeaders(codexVersion),
   106				VersionFields: clientidentity.VersionFields{
   107					CLIVersion: codexVersion,
   108				},
   109				TLSProfileName: clientidentity.TLSProfileCodexCLIDefault,
   110			},
   111		})
   112	}
   113	
   114	func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchVersions(ctx context.Context) (claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion string) {
   115		var wg sync.WaitGroup
   116		var claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer string
   117		var claudeErr, codexErr error
   118	
   119		wg.Add(2)
   120	
   121		go func() {
   122			defer wg.Done()
   123			claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, claudeErr = s.fetchClaudeVersions(ctx)
   124		}()
   125	
   126		go func() {
   127			defer wg.Done()
   128			codexVer, codexErr = s.fetchCodexVersion(ctx)
   129		}()
   130	
   131		wg.Wait()
   132	
   133		if claudeErr != nil || codexErr != nil {
   134			slog.Warn("version_fetcher_discard_update", "claude_error", claudeErr, "codex_error", codexErr)
   135			return "", "", ""
   136		}
   137	
   138		return claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, codexVer
   139	}
   140	
   141	func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
   142		cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
   143		if err != nil {
   144			return "", "", err
   145		}
   146	
   147		sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
   148		if err == nil {
   149			return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
   150		}
   151	
   152		sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
   153		if err != nil {
   154			return "", "", err
   155		}
   156	
   157		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
   158	}
   159	
   160	func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
   161		req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
   162		if err != nil {
   163			return "", err
   164		}
   165		req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
   166		req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
   167	
   168		resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
   169		if err != nil {
   170			return "", err
   171		}
   172		defer resp.Body.Close()
   173	
   174		if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
   175			return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
   176		}
   177	
   178		var release struct {
   179			TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
   180			Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
   181		}
   182		if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
   183			return "", err
   184		}
   185		if release.Prerelease {
   186			return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
   187		}
   188	
   189		version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
   190		if err != nil {
   191			return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
   192		}
   193		return version, nil
   194	}
   195	
   196	func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
   197		url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
   198		req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
   199		if err != nil {
   200			return "", err
   201		}
   202		req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
   203	
   204		resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
   205		if err != nil {
   206			return "", err
   207		}
   208		defer resp.Body.Close()
   209	
   210		if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
   211			return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
   212		}
   213	
   214		var data struct {
   215			DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
   216		}
   217		if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
   218			return "", err
   219		}
   220	
   221		latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
   222		if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
   223			return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
   224		}
   225	
   226		version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
   227		if err != nil {
   228			return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
   229		}
   230		return version, nil
   231	}
   232	
   233	func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
   234		url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
   235		req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
   236		if err != nil {
   237			return "", err
   238		}
   239		req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
   240	
   241		resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
   242		if err != nil {
   243			return "", err
   244		}
   245		defer resp.Body.Close()
   246	
   247		if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
   248			return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
   249		}
   250	
   251		var data struct {
   252			Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
   253		}
   254		if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
   255			return "", err
   256		}
   257	
   258		sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
   259		if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
   260			return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
   261		}
   262	
   263		version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
   264		if err != nil {
   265			return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
   266		}
   267		return version, nil
   268	}
   269	
   270	func (s *VersionFetcherService) buildClaudeHeaders(cliVer, sdkVer string) map[string]string {
   271		return map[string]string{
   272			"User-Agent":                  "claude-cli/" + cliVer + " (external, cli)",
   273			"X-Stainless-Package-Version": sdkVer,
   274			"X-App":                       "cli",
   275		}
   276	}
   277	
   278	func (s *VersionFetcherService) buildCodexHeaders(cliVer string) map[string]string {
   279		return map[string]string{
   280			"User-Agent": "codex_cli_rs/" + cliVer + " (Ubuntu 22.4.0; x86_64) xterm-256color",
   281			"originator": "codex_cli_rs",
   282		}
   283	}
   284	
   285	func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
   286		if s != nil && s.client != nil {
   287			return s.client
   288		}
   289		return http.DefaultClient
   290	}
   291	
   292	var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
   293	
   294	func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
   295		token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
   296		if token == "" {
   297			return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
   298		}
   299		if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
   300			return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
   301		}
   302		return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
   303	}

   191	func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
   192		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
   193			switch r.URL.Path {
   194			case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
   195				_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
   196			case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
   197				http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
   198			case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
   199				_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
   200			default:
   201				http.NotFound(w, r)
   202			}
   203		})
   204		defer server.Close()
   205	
   206		cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
   207		require.NoError(t, err)
   208		assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
   209		assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)
   210	}

 func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchVersions(ctx context.Context) (claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion string) {

-	return "", "", ""

+
+	wg.Add(2)
+
+	go func() {
+		defer wg.Done()
+		claudeVer, claudeSDKVer, claudeErr = s.fetchClaudeVersions(ctx)
+	}()
+

+		defer wg.Done()

+	}()

+		slog.Warn("version_fetcher_discard_update", "claude_error", claudeErr, "codex_error", codexErr)
+		return "", "", ""
+	}

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
+	if err == nil {
+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}

 	}
 }
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) httpClient() *http.Client {
+	if s != nil && s.client != nil {
+		return s.client
+	}
+	return http.DefaultClient
+}
+
+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)
+}

codex
已完成 R1 step2：`fetchVersions` 从占位改为真实联网拉取，并补了 mock HTTP 单测。

改动范围只在两个文件：

- [version_fetcher_service.go](/mnt/x/project/sub2api/backend/internal/service/version_fetcher_service.go:114)
  - 实现 `fetchVersions`：并行拉取 Claude 版本组与 Codex 版本；任一失败整体丢弃，保持旧快照。
  - 实现 `fetchClaudeVersions`：先取 npm `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` latest，再优先解析该版本包内 `@anthropic-ai/sdk` 依赖；失败才兜底 npm `@anthropic-ai/sdk` latest。
  - 实现 `fetchCodexVersion`：调用 GitHub `openai/codex/releases/latest`，带 `User-Agent`，解析 `tag_name`，过滤 prerelease，trim `v`。
  - 实现 `fetchNPMLatest` 与 `fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency`：处理非 200、无 latest、无 sdk dependency、ctx 超时、`^`/`~`/`v`/UA 式版本提取。
  - `buildCodexHeaders` 同步修正为 `codex_cli_rs/<ver> (Ubuntu 22.4.0; x86_64) xterm-256color`，保持 UA 前缀与 `originator=codex_cli_rs` 同族。

- [version_fetcher_service_test.go](/mnt/x/project/sub2api/backend/internal/service/version_fetcher_service_test.go:32)
  - `TestFetchNPMLatest`：正常、404、无 latest、prerelease、ctx 超时。
  - `TestFetchCodexVersion`：正常、trim `v`、prerelease flag、prerelease tag、404。
  - `TestFetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency`：正常、trim `^`、trim `~`、无 sdk dependency、404。
  - `TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest`：claude-code 包依赖解析失败后兜底 sdk latest。
  - `TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails`：任一源失败整体返回空。
  - `TestFetchAndUpdateBuildsConsistentCodexIdentity`：更新后 codex 版本、UA、originator 一致。

错误处理现在是：

- npm / GitHub 非 `200` 返回错误。
- 无 `dist-tags.latest` 返回错误。
- 无 `@anthropic-ai/sdk` dependency 返回错误并触发 sdk latest 兜底。
- prerelease / build metadata 版本拒绝。
- ctx 超时透传给调用方。
- `fetchVersions` 看到 Claude 组或 Codex 任一失败就返回三个空串，不做半更新，并打一条 warn 日志。

验证结果：

```bash
cd backend
go test ./internal/service -run TestFetch -v
```

结果：通过，`ok github.com/Wei-Shaw/sub2api/internal/service 0.203s`。

额外说明：AGENTS 里要求 GitNexus impact / detect_changes，但当前环境没有 GitNexus MCP，仓库也没有 `.gitnexus/run.cjs` 或 `.claude/skills/gitnexus`，所以无法执行。手动影响范围判断为低风险：`fetchVersions` 原本是占位，调用链只在 `VersionFetcherService.fetchAndUpdate -> registry.Swap` 后台更新路径内。当前工作树已有大量非本次改动，我只修改了上述两个后端 service 文件。

 func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchVersions(ctx context.Context) (claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion string) {

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeVersions(ctx context.Context) (cliVersion, sdkVersion string, err error) {
+	cliVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx, cliVersion)
+	if err == nil {
+		return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+	}
+
+	sdkVersion, err = s.fetchNPMLatest(ctx, "@anthropic-ai/sdk")
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", "", err
+	}
+
+	return cliVersion, sdkVersion, nil
+}

+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchCodexVersion(ctx context.Context) (string, error) {
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, s.codexURL, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/vnd.github.v3+json")
+	req.Header.Set("User-Agent", "sub2api-version-fetcher")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("github API status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var release struct {
+		TagName    string `json:"tag_name"`
+		Prerelease bool   `json:"prerelease"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&release); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	if release.Prerelease {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("latest release is prerelease")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(release.TagName)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid codex release tag %q: %w", release.TagName, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
 }
 
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchNPMLatest(ctx context.Context, pkg string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/" + pkg
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm registry status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		DistTags map[string]string `json:"dist-tags"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	latest, ok := data.DistTags["latest"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(latest) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no latest tag")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(latest)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid npm latest %q: %w", latest, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}
+
+func (s *VersionFetcherService) fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency(ctx context.Context, cliVersion string) (string, error) {
+	url := strings.TrimRight(s.npmURL, "/") + "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/" + cliVersion
+	req, err := http.NewRequestWithContext(ctx, http.MethodGet, url, nil)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	req.Header.Set("Accept", "application/json")
+
+	resp, err := s.httpClient().Do(req)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+	defer resp.Body.Close()
+
+	if resp.StatusCode != http.StatusOK {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("npm package status %d", resp.StatusCode)
+	}
+
+	var data struct {
+		Dependencies map[string]string `json:"dependencies"`
+	}
+	if err := json.NewDecoder(resp.Body).Decode(&data); err != nil {
+		return "", err
+	}
+
+	sdkVer, ok := data.Dependencies["@anthropic-ai/sdk"]
+	if !ok || strings.TrimSpace(sdkVer) == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no sdk dependency")
+	}
+
+	version, err := extractStableVersion(sdkVer)
+	if err != nil {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("invalid sdk dependency %q: %w", sdkVer, err)
+	}
+	return version, nil
+}

+}
+
+var versionTokenPattern = regexp.MustCompile(`v?\d+\.\d+\.\d+(?:[-+][0-9A-Za-z.-]+)?`)
+
+func extractStableVersion(value string) (string, error) {
+	token := versionTokenPattern.FindString(strings.TrimSpace(value))
+	if token == "" {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("no semver token")
+	}
+	if strings.ContainsAny(token, "-+") {
+		return "", fmt.Errorf("prerelease or build metadata version")
+	}
+	return strings.TrimPrefix(token, "v"), nil
+}

+func TestFetchNPMLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	t.Run("returns latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+			assert.Equal(t, "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code", r.URL.Path)
+			assert.Equal(t, "application/json", r.Header.Get("Accept"))
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		got, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.NoError(t, err)
+		assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", got)
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects non 200", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
+			http.Error(w, "not found", http.StatusNotFound)
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.Error(t, err)
+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "npm registry status 404")
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects missing latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"beta":"3.0.0-beta.1"}}`))
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")
+		require.Error(t, err)
+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "no latest tag")
+	})
+
+	t.Run("rejects prerelease latest", func(t *testing.T) {
+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, _ *http.Request) {
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"3.0.0-beta.1"}}`))
+		})
+		defer server.Close()
+
+		_, err := svc.fetchNPMLatest(context.Background(), "@anthropic-ai/claude-code")

+		assert.Contains(t, err.Error(), "prerelease")
+	})

+		svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {

+			w.WriteHeader(http.StatusGatewayTimeout)

+		defer server.Close()
+

+func TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			http.Error(w, "missing package metadata", http.StatusNotFound)
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/sdk":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"0.62.0"}}`))
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	cliVersion, sdkVersion, err := svc.fetchClaudeVersions(context.Background())
+	require.NoError(t, err)
+	assert.Equal(t, "2.1.161", cliVersion)
+	assert.Equal(t, "0.62.0", sdkVersion)
+}

+func TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails(t *testing.T) {
+	svc, server := newVersionFetcherTestService(t, func(w http.ResponseWriter, r *http.Request) {
+		switch r.URL.Path {
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dist-tags":{"latest":"2.1.161"}}`))
+		case "/@anthropic-ai/claude-code/2.1.161":
+			_, _ = w.Write([]byte(`{"dependencies":{"@anthropic-ai/sdk":"^0.62.0"}}`))
+		case "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest":
+			http.Error(w, "github outage", http.StatusBadGateway)
+		default:
+			http.NotFound(w, r)
+		}
+	})
+	defer server.Close()
+
+	claudeVersion, claudeSDKVersion, codexVersion := svc.fetchVersions(context.Background())
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, claudeSDKVersion)
+	assert.Empty(t, codexVersion)
+}

+func newVersionFetcherTestService(t *testing.T, handler http.HandlerFunc) (*VersionFetcherService, *httptest.Server) {
+	t.Helper()
+
+	server := httptest.NewServer(handler)
+	svc := NewVersionFetcherService(clientidentity.NewRegistry(), &config.Config{})
+	svc.client = server.Client()
+	svc.npmURL = server.URL
+	svc.codexURL = server.URL + "/repos/openai/codex/releases/latest"
+	return svc, server
+}

改动范围只在两个文件：

- [version_fetcher_service.go](/mnt/x/project/sub2api/backend/internal/service/version_fetcher_service.go:114)
  - 实现 `fetchVersions`：并行拉取 Claude 版本组与 Codex 版本；任一失败整体丢弃，保持旧快照。
  - 实现 `fetchClaudeVersions`：先取 npm `@anthropic-ai/claude-code` latest，再优先解析该版本包内 `@anthropic-ai/sdk` 依赖；失败才兜底 npm `@anthropic-ai/sdk` latest。
  - 实现 `fetchCodexVersion`：调用 GitHub `openai/codex/releases/latest`，带 `User-Agent`，解析 `tag_name`，过滤 prerelease，trim `v`。
  - 实现 `fetchNPMLatest` 与 `fetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency`：处理非 200、无 latest、无 sdk dependency、ctx 超时、`^`/`~`/`v`/UA 式版本提取。
  - `buildCodexHeaders` 同步修正为 `codex_cli_rs/<ver> (Ubuntu 22.4.0; x86_64) xterm-256color`，保持 UA 前缀与 `originator=codex_cli_rs` 同族。

- [version_fetcher_service_test.go](/mnt/x/project/sub2api/backend/internal/service/version_fetcher_service_test.go:32)
  - `TestFetchNPMLatest`：正常、404、无 latest、prerelease、ctx 超时。
  - `TestFetchCodexVersion`：正常、trim `v`、prerelease flag、prerelease tag、404。
  - `TestFetchClaudeCodeSDKDependency`：正常、trim `^`、trim `~`、无 sdk dependency、404。
  - `TestFetchClaudeVersionsFallsBackToSDKLatest`：claude-code 包依赖解析失败后兜底 sdk latest。
  - `TestFetchVersionsDiscardsWhenAnySourceFails`：任一源失败整体返回空。
  - `TestFetchAndUpdateBuildsConsistentCodexIdentity`：更新后 codex 版本、UA、originator 一致。

错误处理现在是：

- npm / GitHub 非 `200` 返回错误。
- 无 `dist-tags.latest` 返回错误。
- 无 `@anthropic-ai/sdk` dependency 返回错误并触发 sdk latest 兜底。
- prerelease / build metadata 版本拒绝。
- ctx 超时透传给调用方。
- `fetchVersions` 看到 Claude 组或 Codex 任一失败就返回三个空串，不做半更新，并打一条 warn 日志。

验证结果：

```bash
cd backend
go test ./internal/service -run TestFetch -v
```
